if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '3e5dab2ea8a8d4f9a0600de60503b8bfad3fdf9f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3e5dab2ea8a8d4f9a0600de60503b8bfad3fdf9f') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '2bdf65733d8b5e86d3b32c1c6965e06d6ebbcbd4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3e5dab2ea8a8d4f9a0600de60503b8bfad3fdf9f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd') !== 'e0ef6663a98bb1745783872375dfe713446f1f66') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/box_texts/box_texts.psd');
		}
	}
}
